</script><script>function configure_navbar_search(navbar_item_list, name_col, acronym_col) {
  var jquery_autocomplete_data = [];

  // add acronyms to autocomplete data list
  for (var item in navbar_item_list) {
    var acronym = $.trim(navbar_item_list[item][acronym_col]);
    var entry = { value: acronym, data: item };
    jquery_autocomplete_data.push(entry);
  }

  // add item names to autocomplete data list
  for (var item in navbar_item_list) {
    var name = $.trim(navbar_item_list[item][name_col]);
    var entry = { value: name, data: item };
    jquery_autocomplete_data.push(entry);
  }

  // initialize autocomplete functionality on navbar search
  var autocomplete_config = {
    lookup: jquery_autocomplete_data,
    triggerSelectOnValidInput: false,
    autoSelectFirst: true,
    onSelect: function (suggestion) {
      window.location.href = '/item/' + suggestion.data;
    }
  };
  $('#navbar_search_box').autocomplete(autocomplete_config);
}</script><script src="/js/item.js"></script></html>
